<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>SALT LAKE CITY, March 13, 2023</b> -- Clene Inc. (Nasdaq: CLNN) (along with its subsidiaries, &#8220;Clene&#8221;) and its wholly owned subsidiary Clene Nanomedicine Inc., a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on revolutionizing the treatment of neurodegenerative diseases, today announced its full year 2022 financial results and provided recent operating highlights for the clinical programs in ALS and MS.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&#8220;We had an extremely productive year during which we generated consistent positive results from our clinical programs in ALS and MS that have helped advance both programs toward the next regulatory milestones. The initial placebo-controlled double-blinded Phase 2 RESCUE-ALS results were strengthened further with evidence of a survival benefit and preserved function at one year and beyond. The HEALEY ALS Platform Trial demonstrated consistent evidence of delayed time to ALS clinical worsening at six months in addition to a survival benefit,&#8221; said Rob Etherington, President and CEO of Clene. &#8220;Results from our ALS clinical trials taken together along with significant Phase 2 findings of improvements in clinical outcomes, brain structure, and enhanced visual system signaling in stable MS patients from the VISIONARY-MS trial, have taught us of CNM-Au8&#8217;s efficacy in multiple therapeutic areas. The totality of the clinical and paraclinical data are robust. In 2023, we will work to advance regulatory discussions with FDA on both ALS and MS and pursue partnering opportunities for the MS indication.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Fourth Quarter 2022 and Recent Operating Highlights</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><i><b>CNM-Au8, a gold nanocrystal suspension, for the treatment of ALS</b></i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">New clinical improvement data from the HEALEY ALS Platform Trial (n=120 CNM-Au8 treated patients and 164 placebo-treated patients), led by the Sean M. Healey &amp; AMG Center for ALS at Massachusetts General Hospital demonstrated a 74% decreased risk (lower hazard) of the composite endpoint of time to ALS clinical worsening (p = 0.035) as well as statistically significant and directional trends across all prespecified time to clinical worsening event analyses:</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 10pt;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">98% decreased risk (lower hazard) of death or permanently assisted ventilation (p= 0.028)</td>
		</tr>
		<tr style="font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">74% decreased risk of feeding tube placement (p= 0.035)</td>
		</tr>
		<tr style="font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">63% decreased risk of assisted ventilation (p= 0.058)</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">New clinical results showing preserved ALS patient functional score (ALSFRS-R) and delayed time to clinical worsening from the most recent 12-month data cut of the OLE of the Phase 2 RESCUE ALS trial in people with early ALS, specifically:</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 10pt;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">Statistically significant difference in ALSFRS-R slope from day 1 (randomization) to week 48: among participants originally randomized to active compared to participants originally randomized to placebo (p=0.0159)</td>
		</tr>
		<tr style="font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">Statistically significant difference in ALSFRS-R slope from week 60 to week 120 comparing participants originally randomized to active or placebo (p=0.0057).</td>
		</tr>
		<tr style="font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">The risk of ALS progression was less than half for those originally receiving CNM-Au8 compared to those originally receiving placebo (p=0.0494).</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">Clene continues to support two expanded access programs providing CNM-Au8 treatment at four clinical sites to more than 50 participants with ALS and is presently expanding one EAP to include multiple centers across the U.S. and enroll up to 200 additional participants. The company plans to meet with the U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA) in an end of Phase 2 meeting during the third quarter of 2023 to discuss the regulatory path forward for CNM-Au8 in ALS.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left"><i><b>CNM-Au8 for the treatment of MS</b></i></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">New data from the VISIONARY MS trial from MRI and VEP provide evidence of improved information signaling from the eye to the brain&#8217;s visual cortex and improved brain neuronal structural integrity and decreased brain deterioration further supporting primary and secondary results shared in August 2022, including:</p>

<p style="text-align: justify; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 10pt;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">Multi-focal Visual Evoked Potential (mf-VEP) findings provide evidence of improved information transmission in the visual system (from the eye to the visual cortex) with increased amplitude signal suggesting previously impaired neurons subsequently increase information transmission following CNM-Au8 treatment, supporting improved axonal integrity:</td>
		</tr>

</table>

		</tr>
		<tr style="font-size: 10pt;">
			<td style="width: 8%; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 3%; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9675;</td>
			<td style="width: 89%; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">mf-VEP amplitude percent change across both eyes &#8211; Week 48 LS mean difference: 7.9%, 95% CI: 1.4% to 14.4%, p=0.0184</td>
		</tr>

			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">MRI findings provide evidence of brain neuronal structural integrity assessed by diffusion tensor imaging (DTI) that demonstrated statistically significant results for key metrics of axonal integrity and white matter integrity, independent of an immunomodulatory effect, with:</td>
		</tr>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Full Year 2022 Financial Results</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Clene&#8217;s cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities totaled&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="355368" data-tblv="55" id="led355368F2023291678402864007" originalfact="$ 23,315,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000" style="font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">$23.3 million</a>&nbsp;as of <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555577390">December 31, 2022</a>, compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x2" data-tblname="355368" data-tblv="55" id="led355368F2023291678402869827" originalfact="$ 50,288,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000" style="font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">$50.3 million</a>&nbsp;as of <a data-tblloc="6x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555672684">December 31, 2021</a>. Clene expects that its resources as of <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555591251">December 31, 2022</a>, will be sufficient to fund its operations into the third quarter of 2023.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">Research and development expenses were <a data-tblloc="8x5" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402887420" originalfact="$31,920,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$31.9 million</a>&nbsp;for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555598233">December 31, 2022</a>, compared to <a data-tblloc="8x6" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402894468" originalfact="$28,416,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$28.4 million</a>&nbsp;for the same period in <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555689097">2021</a>. The year-over-year increase was primarily related to the development of CNM-Au8 and CNM-ZnAg, rent expense for the newly-leased facility in Elkton, Maryland, and personnel, partially offset by decreased stock-based compensation and depreciation expense.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">General and administrative expenses were <a data-tblloc="9x5" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402907135" originalfact="$16,936,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$16.9 million</a>&nbsp;for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555606648">December 31, 2022</a>, compared to <a data-tblloc="9x6" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402913567" originalfact="$21,996,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$22.0 million</a>&nbsp;for the same period in <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555698575">2021</a>. The year-over-year decrease was primarily attributable to lower finance and accounting fees, legal expenses and stock-based compensation, offset by increased personnel expenses.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">Total other income (expense) was <a data-tblloc="21x5" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402934922" originalfact="$18,491,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$18.5 million</a>&nbsp;for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555612281">December 31, 2022</a>, compared to <a data-tblloc="21x6" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402940605" originalfact="$39,810,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$39.8 million</a>&nbsp;for the same period in <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555702807">2021</a>. The year-over-year decrease was primarily attributable to a decrease in the change in the fair value of the Clene and initial shareholder contingent earn-out liability, an increase in interest expense due to increasing interest rates during 2022, and&nbsp;a decrease in the change in the fair value of the common stock warrant liability; offset by an increase in research and development credits received in 2022.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Clene reported a net loss of <a data-tblloc="24x5" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402960380" originalfact="$29,918,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$29.9 million</a>, or <a data-tblloc="32x5" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402976093">$0.46</a>&nbsp;per share, for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555626621">December 31, 2022</a>, compared to a net loss of <a data-tblloc="24x6" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402968661" originalfact="$9,740,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$9.7 million</a>, or <a data-tblloc="32x6" data-tblname="328565" data-tblv="55" id="led328565F2023291678402982291">$0.16</a>&nbsp;per share, for the same period in <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="324292" data-tblv="55" id="led324292F20232111678555713490">2021</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left"><b>About Clene</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Clene is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on revolutionizing the treatment of neurodegenerative disease by targeting energetic failure, an underlying cause of many neurological diseases. The company is based in Salt Lake City, Utah, with R&amp;D and manufacturing operations in Maryland. For more information, please visit www.clene.com or follow us on <u>Twitter</u>, <u>LinkedIn</u> and <u>Facebook</u>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left"><b>About CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:pt">&#174;</sup></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">CNM-Au8 is an oral suspension of gold nanocrystals developed to restore neuronal health and function by increasing energy production and utilization. The catalytically active nanocrystals of CNM-Au8 drive critical cellular energy producing reactions that enable neuroprotection and remyelination by increasing neuronal and glial resilience to disease-relevant stressors. CNM-Au8&#174; is a federally registered trademark of Clene Nanomedicine, Inc.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
